<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'font-f=
amily:
Calibri'>1.</span><span style=3D'font-family:"Microsoft YaHei"'>按下</spa=
n><span
style=3D'font-family:Calibri'>F1</span><span style=3D'font-family:"Microsof=
t YaHei"'>获得有关</span><span
style=3D'font-family:Calibri'>IDLE</span><span style=3D'font-family:"Micros=
oft YaHei"'>的帮助</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>2.&gt;&gt;&gt;1/2</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span>0</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>3.&gt;&gt;&gt;1.0/2</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span>0.5</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US>参与除法的两个数中有一个数为浮点数</span><spa=
n lang=3Dzh-CN>，则运算结果也为浮点数</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US>4.如果希望python只执行普通的除法</span><span lang=
=3Dzh-CN>，那么可以在程序前加上</span><span
lang=3Den-US>:</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>from _future_ import division</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;1/2</=
p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>0=
.5</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span>在这种情况=
</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>，使用双斜线又可以恢复取整除法</span><span lang=
=3Den-US>:</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;1 // =
2</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>0=
</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>5.幂运算符:</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;2**3</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>8<=
/p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;-3**2</=
p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>-9=
</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;(-3)**2=
</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>9<=
/p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>注意</span><span =
lang=3Dzh-CN>：幂运算符</span><span
lang=3Den-US>(**)</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>比取反(</span><span lang=3Den=
-US>-)的优先级高</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US>6.变量名可以包括字母</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>、数=
、下划线。变量不能以数字开头。</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>7.pow(2,3)等价于2**3</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>8.abs:取绝对值函数</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;abs(-10=
)</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>10=
</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>9.round函数:把浮点数四舍五入为最接近的整数值=
</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;round(1=
.0/2.0)</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>1.0</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US>10.模块</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>：把模块导入到Python=
以增强其功能的扩展。</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>     </span></span><span
style=3D'color:#E84C22' lang=3Dzh-CN>使用</span><span style=3D'color:#E84=
C22'
lang=3Den-US>import导入模块</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>。</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US>11.floor函数</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>：向下取整函数<=
/span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;import =
math</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;math.fl=
oor(32.9)
#格式</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>：</span><span lang=3Den-US>模块. 函=
(参数)</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>32=
.0</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>12. from 模块 import 函数</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>     </span>使用了这=
形式的import的命令</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>，就可以直接使用函数，而不需要模块名作为=
缀。</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in'><img src=3D"file6000.files/image=
001.png"
width=3D319 height=3D66 alt=3D"from math &#10;sqrt (9) &#10;import &#10;sqr=
t &#10;3.0 "></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt'><span lang=3Dzh-CN>提示：可以使用变量来引用=
数</span><span lang=3Den-US>(</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>或者</span><span lang=3Den-US>Python</span><span lang=3Dzh-C=
N>中大多数的对象</span><span
lang=3Den-US>)</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>。比如，通过</span><span lang=
=3Den-US>foo=3Dmath.sqrt</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>进行赋值，然后就可以使用</span><span lang=3Den-US>=
foo</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>来计算平方根了</span><span
lang=3Den-US>:foo(4)</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>的结果为</span><span lang=
=3Den-US>2.0</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>13.cmath模块:使用cmath模块来对负数求根</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;import =
cmath</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>&gt;&gt;&gt;cmath.s=
qrt(-1)</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>1j=
</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>14._future_模块</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>通过_future_模=
</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>，可以导入那些在未来会成为标准Python组成部=
的新特性。</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>15.字符串</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;”Hello,world!”</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>‘Hello,world!’</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;’Hello,world!’</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>‘Hello,world!’</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;”Let’s go!”</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>“Let’s go!”</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;’Let’s go!’</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>错误</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;’Let\’s go!’</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>“Let’s go!”</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;’”Hello,world!”she said’=
</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>’”Hello,world!”she said’</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>16.使用+拼接字符串</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US>17.字符串表示</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>，</span><span la=
ng=3Den-US>str和repr</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt;color:red'><span style=3D'font-weight:bold' lang=3Den-US>s=
tr</span><span
style=3D'font-weight:bold' lang=3Dzh-CN>函数：把值转换为合理形=
的</span><span style=3D'font-weight:
bold;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline' lang=3Dzh-CN>字符串</s=
pan></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt;color:red'><span style=3D'font-weight:bold'>repr函数：=
建一个字符串，以合法的Python表达式的形式来表示值</sp=
an></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11.=
0pt'
lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;print str(“Hello,world!”)</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11.=
0pt'
lang=3Den-US>Hello,world!</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11.=
0pt'
lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;print repr(“Hello,world!”)</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11.=
0pt'
lang=3Den-US>‘Hello,world!’</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;print str(10000L)</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>10000</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&nbsp;</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt'><span lang=3Dzh-CN>总结，</span><span lang=3Den-US>str=
</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>和</span><span lang=3Den-US>repr</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>是=
将</span><span
lang=3Den-US>Python</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>值转换为字符串的</span=
><span lang=3Den-US>3</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>种方法。函数</span><span lang=3Den-US>str</span><span la=
ng=3Dzh-CN>让字符串更易于阅读，而</span><span
lang=3Den-US>repr</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>则把</span><span lang=3Den-US>=
 </span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>字符串转换为合法的</span><span lang=3Den-US>Python</s=
pan><span lang=3Dzh-CN>表达式。</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt;color:red'><span style=3D'font-weight:bold'>注意：不=
以将字符串和数字直接相加。</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>18.input和raw_input</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt'><span lang=3Den-US>input会假设用户输入的是合法=
的Python表达式</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>。就例如在输入一个字符串的时候要输入</span><=
span lang=3Den-US>”汪子豪”</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>，竟然要我们输双引号。</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'>&nbs=
p;</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-size:11.0pt'><span
style=3D'font-family:"Microsoft YaHei"' lang=3Dzh-CN>raw</span><span
style=3D'font-family:Calibri' lang=3Den-US>_input</span><span style=3D'font=
-family:
"Microsoft YaHei"' lang=3Den-US>函数把所有的输入当作原始数据<=
/span><span style=3D'font-family:
"Microsoft YaHei"' lang=3Dzh-CN>，然后将其放入字符串。</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in'><img src=3D"file6000.files/image=

width=3D600 height=3D276
alt=3D"hello world.py - world.py (2.7.13) &#10;File Edit Format Ryo—ption=

. py &#10;Hello, world! &#10;What is your name? &#10;Hello, ! "></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'><span
lang=3Den-US>19.长字符串</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>：三个单引号’=
</span><span lang=3Den-US>’’</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>。长字符串可以换行</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in'><img src=3D"file6000.files/image=
005.png"
width=3D284 height=3D168></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>20.原始字符串几个注意点:</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt'><span lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;print ‘Hello\n</span><sp=
an
lang=3Dzh-CN>world</span><span lang=3Den-US>!’</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>Hello</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>World!</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;print ‘C:\\nowhere\\file’</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>C:\nowhere\file</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>&gt;&gt;&gt;print r’C:\nowhere’</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt' lang=3Den-US>C:\nowhere</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt'><span lang=3Den-US>注</span><span lang=3Dzh-CN>：原始=
字符串以r开头，可以基本原样输出字符串。</span><span
lang=3Den-US><span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>          </span></s=
pan></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";font-size:11.0pt'
lang=3Den-US>21.</p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt'><span lang=3Den-US>math.ceil(number) #</span><span lang=
=3Dzh-CN>返回数的上入整数，返回值的类型为浮点数</span></=
p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt'><span lang=3Den-US>math.floor(number) #</span><span lang=
=3Dzh-CN>返回数的下舍整数，返回值的类型为浮点数</span></=
p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt'><span lang=3Den-US>math.sqrt(number) #</span><span lang=
=3Dzh-CN>返回平方根，不适用于负数</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in;font-family:"Microsoft YaHei";
font-size:11.0pt'><span lang=3Den-US>round(number[,ndigits]) #</span><span
lang=3Dzh-CN>根据给定的精度对数字进行四舍五入</span></p>

<p style=3D'margin:0in;margin-left:.375in'><img src=3D"file6000.files/image=
006.png"
width=3D323 height=3D186
alt=3D"8.0 &#10;math &#10;Import &#10;math. ceil (8. 6) &#10;math. floor (8=
.6) &#10;math. sqrt (8. 6) &#10;2. 932575659723036 &#10;round (8.6) &#10;9.=
0 "></p>
